DROP TABLE Products;
DROP TABLE Customers;
DROP TABLE Categories;
DROP TABLE Payment_Method;
DROP TABLE Locations;
DROP TABLE Areas;
DROP TABLE Employees;
--DROP TABLE Contacts;
DROP TABLE Orders;
DROP TABLE Order_Details;
DROP sequence CONTACTS_SEQ;

/

CREATE TABLE Products (
	category_id INT,
	product_id INT,
	product_name varchar2(256),
	price DECIMAL(10,4),
	hot CHAR(1),
	vegetarian CHAR(1),
	CONSTRAINT PRODUCTS_PK PRIMARY KEY (product_id),
  CONSTRAINT cons_Products_hot CHECK (hot IN ('1','0')),
  CONSTRAINT cons_Products_vegetarian CHECK (vegetarian IN ('1','0'))
);

CREATE TABLE Categories (
	category_id INT,
	categories_name varchar2 (50),
	constraint CATEGORIES_PK PRIMARY KEY (category_id));

CREATE TABLE Customers (
	customer_id INT,
	customer_name varchar2 (200),
	has_card CHAR(1),
	CONSTRAINT CUSTOMERS_PK PRIMARY KEY (customer_id),
  CONSTRAINT cons_Customers_has_card CHECK (has_card IN ('1','0')));

CREATE TABLE Payment_Method (
	payment_method_id INT,
	payment_method_name varchar2 (50),
	constraint PAYMENT_METHOD_PK PRIMARY KEY (payment_method_id));

CREATE TABLE Locations (
	location_id INT,
	street varchar2 (100),
	house_number varchar2 (10),
	area_id INT,
	constraint LOCATIONS_PK PRIMARY KEY (location_id));

CREATE TABLE Areas (
	area_id INT,
	areas_name varchar2 (30),
	constraint AREAS_PK PRIMARY KEY (area_id));

CREATE TABLE Employees (
	employee_id INT,
	employee_name varchar (1000),
	chief_id INT,
	start_date DATE,
	street varchar (1000),
	house_number varchar (1000),	
	phone varchar (1000),
	apartment INT,
	constraint EMPLOYEES_PK PRIMARY KEY (employee_id));

CREATE TABLE Orders (
	order_id INT,
	payment_method_id INT,
	employee_id INT,	
	customer_id INT,
	ex_comment varchar2 (1000),
	location_id INT,
	delivery_date DATE,
	order_date DATE,
	end_date DATE,
	constraint ORDERS_PK PRIMARY KEY (order_id));

CREATE TABLE Order_Details (
	product_id INT,
	order_id INT,
	quantity INT,	
  CONSTRAINT ORDER_DETAILS_PK PRIMARY KEY (product_id, order_id)	
);
/
select table_name from user_tables;
